tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nickname(s).

tranquility.anonops.net -> anon-ymous: Channel .#lorrainconus. isn't registered.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nickname(s).

tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nickname(s).

tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: .ChanServ. allows you to register and control various
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: aspects of channels.  ChanServ can often prevent
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: malicious users from "taking over" channels by limiting
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: who is allowed channel operator privileges.  Available
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: commands are listed below; to use them, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: ./msg ChanServ .command...  For more information on a
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: specific command, type ./msg ChanServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     REGISTER   Register a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     SET        Set channel options and information
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     SOP        Modify the list of SOP users
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     AOP        Modify the list of AOP users
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     HOP        Maintains the HOP (HalfOP) list for a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     VOP        Maintains the VOP (VOicePeople) list for a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     ACCESS     Modify the list of privileged users
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     LEVELS     Redefine the meanings of access levels
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     SENDPASS   Help retrieve lost passwords
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     CLEAR      Tells ChanServ to clear certain settings on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     OWNER      Gives you owner status on channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DEOWNER    Removes your owner status on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     PROTECT    Protects a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DEPROTECT  Deprotects a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     OP         Gives Op status to a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DEOP       Deops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     HALFOP     Halfops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DEHALFOP   Dehalfops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     VOICE      Voices a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     DEVOICE    Devoices a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     GETKEY     Returns the key of the given channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     INVITE     Tells ChanServ to invite you into a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     KICK       Kicks a selected nick from a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     LOGOUT     This command will logout the selected nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     TOPIC      Manipulate the topic of the specified channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     INFO       Lists information about the named registered channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     BAN        Bans a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     UNBAN      Remove all bans preventing you from entering a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     AKICK      Maintain the AutoKick list
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     APPENDTOPIC   Add text to a channels topic
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:     ENFORCE    Enforce various channel modes and set options
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:  SYNC       Give all users the status the access list grants them.
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: Note that any channel which is not used for 30 days
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: (i.e. which no user on the channel's access list enters
tranquility.anonops.net -> ShadowOp: for that period of time) will be automatically dropped.

tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> sleinad: nickname(s).

gtn -> chanserv: help
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: .ChanServ. allows you to register and control various
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: aspects of channels.  ChanServ can often prevent
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: malicious users from "taking over" channels by limiting
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: who is allowed channel operator privileges.  Available
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: commands are listed below; to use them, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: ./msg ChanServ .command...  For more information on a
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn: specific command, type ./msg ChanServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     REGISTER   Register a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     SET        Set channel options and information
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     SOP        Modify the list of SOP users
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     AOP        Modify the list of AOP users
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     HOP        Maintains the HOP (HalfOP) list for a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     VOP        Maintains the VOP (VOicePeople) list for a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     ACCESS     Modify the list of privileged users
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     LEVELS     Redefine the meanings of access levels
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     SENDPASS   Help retrieve lost passwords
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     CLEAR      Tells ChanServ to clear certain settings on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     OWNER      Gives you owner status on channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DEOWNER    Removes your owner status on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     PROTECT    Protects a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DEPROTECT  Deprotects a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     OP         Gives Op status to a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DEOP       Deops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     HALFOP     Halfops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DEHALFOP   Dehalfops a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     VOICE      Voices a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     DEVOICE    Devoices a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     GETKEY     Returns the key of the given channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     INVITE     Tells ChanServ to invite you into a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     KICK       Kicks a selected nick from a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     LOGOUT     This command will logout the selected nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     TOPIC      Manipulate the topic of the specified channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     INFO       Lists information about the named registered channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     BAN        Bans a selected nick on a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     UNBAN      Remove all bans preventing you from entering a channel
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     AKICK      Maintain the AutoKick list
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     APPENDTOPIC   Add text to a channels topic
tranquility.anonops.net -> gtn:     ENFORCE    Enforce various channel modes and set options

K4n0n -> K4n0n: LAGCHK 177475.725
Mircale -> Nickserv: Help
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> Mircale: nickname(s).
Cogitabundus -> Anonymous9: Me though.

Pacotron -> nickserv: help register
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Syntax: .REGISTER .password. .[email]..
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Registers your nickname in the NickServ database.  Once
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: your nick is registered, you can use the .SET. and .ACCESS.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: commands to configure your nick's settings as you like
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: them.  Make sure you remember the password you use when
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: registering - you'll need it to make changes to your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: later.  (Note that .case matters!.  .ANOPE., .Anope., and 
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: .anope. are all different passwords!)
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Guidelines on choosing passwords:
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Passwords should not be easily guessable.  For example,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: using your real name as a password is a bad idea.  Using
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: your nickname as a password is a much worse idea ;) and,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: in fact, NickServ will not allow it.  Also, short
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: passwords are vulnerable to trial-and-error searches, so
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: you should choose a password at least 5 characters long.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Finally, the space character cannot be used in passwords.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: The parameter .email. is optional and will set the email
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: for your nick immediately. However, it may be required
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: on certain networks.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Your privacy is respected; this e-mail won't be given to
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: any third-party person.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: This command also creates a new group for your nickname,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: that will allow you to register other nicks later sharing
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: the same configuration, the same set of memos and the
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: same channel privileges. For more information on this
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: feature, type ./msg NickServ HELP GROUP..

Pacotron -> nickserv: help register
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Syntax: .REGISTER .password. .[email]..
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Registers your nickname in the NickServ database.  Once
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: your nick is registered, you can use the .SET. and .ACCESS.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: commands to configure your nick's settings as you like
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: them.  Make sure you remember the password you use when
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: registering - you'll need it to make changes to your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: later.  (Note that .case matters!.  .ANOPE., .Anope., and 
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: .anope. are all different passwords!)
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Guidelines on choosing passwords:
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Passwords should not be easily guessable.  For example,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: using your real name as a password is a bad idea.  Using
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: your nickname as a password is a much worse idea ;) and,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: in fact, NickServ will not allow it.  Also, short
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: passwords are vulnerable to trial-and-error searches, so
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: you should choose a password at least 5 characters long.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Finally, the space character cannot be used in passwords.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: The parameter .email. is optional and will set the email
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: for your nick immediately. However, it may be required
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: on certain networks.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Your privacy is respected; this e-mail won't be given to
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: any third-party person.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: This command also creates a new group for your nickname,
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: that will allow you to register other nicks later sharing
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: the same configuration, the same set of memos and the
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: same channel privileges. For more information on this
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: feature, type ./msg NickServ HELP GROUP..

Pacotron -> nickserv: help
Psycho -> Psycho: LAGCHK 150075.311
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> Pacotron: nickname(s).

e -> e: 
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: .NickServ. allows you to "register" a nickname and
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: prevent others from using it. The following
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: commands allow for registration and maintenance of
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: nicknames; to use them, type ./msg NickServ .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: For more information on a specific command, type
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: ./msg NickServ HELP .command...
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     REGISTER   Register a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GROUP      Join a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GLIST      Lists all nicknames in your group
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     IDENTIFY   Identify yourself with your password
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     ACCESS     Modify the list of authorized addresses
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     SET        Set options, including kill protection
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     SASET      Set SET-options on another nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     DROP       Cancel the registration of a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     RECOVER    Kill another user who has taken your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     RELEASE    Regain custody of your nick after RECOVER
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     SENDPASS   Forgot your password? Try this
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GHOST      Disconnects a "ghost" IRC session using your nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     ALIST      List channels you have access on
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     INFO       Displays information about a given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     LIST       List all registered nicknames that match a given pattern
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     LOGOUT     Reverses the effect of the IDENTIFY command
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     STATUS     Returns the owner status of the given nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     UPDATE     Updates your current status, i.e. it checks for new memos
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GETPASS    Retrieve the password for a nickname
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GETEMAIL   Matches and returns all users that registered using given email
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     FORBID     Prevents a nickname from being registered
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     SUSPEND    Suspend a given nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     UNSUSPEND  Unsuspend a given nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     OINFO         Add / Del an OperInfo line to a nick
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:     GROUPSWHOIS  Syncs all the swhoises for all nicks in a group
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: Services admins can also drop any nickname without needing
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: to identify for the nick, and may view the access list for
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: any nickname (./msg NickServ ACCESS LIST .nick..).
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: Nicknames that are not used anymore are subject to 
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: the automatic expiration, i.e. they will be deleted
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: after 30 days if not used.
tranquility.anonops.net -> e:  
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: .NOTICE:. This service is intended to provide a way for
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: IRC users to ensure their identity is not compromised.
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: It is .NOT. intended to facilitate "stealing" of
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: nicknames or other malicious actions.  Abuse of NickServ
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: will result in, at minimum, loss of the abused
tranquility.anonops.net -> e: nickname(s).
